TypeError: unhashable type: 'list'

https://rollbar.com/blog/handling-unhashable-type-list-exceptions/

Sets require their items to be hashable. Out of types predefined by Python only the immutable ones, such as strings, numbers, and tuples, are hashable. 
Mutable types, such as lists and dicts, are not hashable because a change of their contents would change the hash and break the lookup code.

In this Patient Data Monitor project, we receive specialty diseases data of patient from data provider. 
As per the requirements that data filters in the pipeline for which we have different notebooks. 
Filtered data will publish in the Redshift which is a database of AWS. As per the business requirements we generate graphs on the ICyte portal. 
As per the logic mentioned in notebook whether data is reflecting or not that we test. Also, 
we check that proper restatement is happening or not in the given notebooks and new changes applied to the data in the pipeline. 
We deal with patient data of specialty pharmacy’s rare diseases. What are the diseases we don’t know because 
as per the HIPPA rule they can’t reveal patient’s private data. We check entire patient journey during this process. 
How business should grow that we show through graph which will be beneficial to the customer.

As per the process we create the TC and Report generates as per the automated data


Patient data QA Ingest Quality Check

How the Patient journey is there in the entire process as per that we generate Longitudinal id, Patient ID
At which stage the End user takes/stops the Theropy/treatment that we can check
How much Total shipment, Dispense which happened that we can see through the graphs

import pandas as pd
df_csv = pd.read_csv(r'C:\Users\reddyma\sample_data\Test\Read_Write_Data\Data\Idorsia tdms.inventory_analytics.csv',
                             converters={i: str for i in range(1000)})
df_csv1 = pd.read_csv(r'Data/Idorsia tdms.inventory_analytics_DB.csv',
                             converters={i: str for i in range(1000)})
lis_dic = df_csv.to_dict('records')
lis_dic1 = df_csv1.to_dict('records')
# print(lis_dic)
# print(lis_dic1)

# print(type(lis_dic))

empty_list = []
empty_list1 = []
# for 1st csv
for ele in lis_dic:
    dic = {}
    week = ele['week']
    channel = ele['channel']
    prod_grp_id = ele['prod_grp_id']
    ecs_qs = ele['ecs_qs']
    trx_cnt = ele['trx_cnt']
    trx_qty = ele['trx_qty']
    build_burn = ele['build_burn']
    demand = ele["demand"]
    keyd = week + '_' + channel + '_' + prod_grp_id
    # trx_cnt, trx_qty, build_burn, demand
    dic[keyd] = {"ecs_qs": ecs_qs,"trx_cnt":trx_cnt, "trx_qty":trx_qty, "build_burn":build_burn, "demand":demand}
    # li.append(keyd)
    empty_list.append(dic)
# print(empty_list)
# for second csv
for ele1 in lis_dic1:
    dic1 = {}
    week = ele1['week']
    channel = ele1['channel']
    prod_grp_id = ele1['prod_grp_id']
    ecs_qs = ele1['ecs_qs']
    trx_cnt = ele1['trx_cnt']
    trx_qty = ele1['trx_qty']
    build_burn = ele1['build_burn']
    demand = ele1["demand"]
    keyd = week + '_' + channel + '_' + prod_grp_id
    dic1[keyd] = {"ecs_qs": ecs_qs,"trx_cnt":trx_cnt, "trx_qty":trx_qty, "build_burn":build_burn, "demand":demand}
    # li.append(keyd)
    empty_list1.append(dic1)
print(empty_list)
# print(empty_list1)
print(empty_list1)
var = []
r = []
for eles in empty_list:
    if eles in empty_list1:
        print(eles)
        ind = empty_list1.index(eles)
        # print(empty_list1(ind))
        for el11, eq in eles.items():

            for el in empty_list1[ind].values():
                print(el)
                if eq['ecs_qs'] == el['ecs_qs'] and eq['trx_cnt'] == el['trx_cnt'] and eq['trx_qty'] == el['trx_qty']:
                    out = "pass"
                    r.append("element is passed")
                    var.append(out)
                # f = eq['ecs_qs']

context.username1 = enter_the_username(row['username'])

login_page.py

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from utilities.configu import *
from PageObjectModule.Locators.locator import *

# class LoginPage:

# def __init__(self):
#     self.driver_chrome = self.driver_chrome
#     self.enter_username = "email"
#     self.enter_password = "pass"
#     self.click_login = "login"
from utilities.urls import DifferentUrl

username_textbox_id = Locator.username_textbox_id
password_textbox_id = Locator.password_textbox_id
login_button_name = Locator.login_button_name
driver_chrome = webdriver.Chrome()
driver_chrome.get(DifferentUrl.url_facebook)

def enter_the_username(username):
    username_input = driver_chrome.find_element(By.ID, username_textbox_id).send_keys(username)
    return username_input


def enter_the_password(password):
    password_input = driver_chrome.find_element(By.ID, password_textbox_id).send_keys(password)
    return password_input


def click_login():
    click_button = driver_chrome.find_element(By.NAME, login_button_name).click()
    return click_button

substatus_utilization_union='''SELECT ic_transaction_id, longitudinal_patient_id, pharmacy_parent_name, brand, referral_date, status_date, status, substatus, ship_date, status_month, status_quarter, status_year, days_in_status, "__metadata_run_id", "__metadata_run_timestamp"
FROM helsinn.substatus_utilization
except
SELECT ic_transaction_id, longitudinal_patient_id, pharmacy_parent_name, brand, referral_date, status_date, status, substatus, ship_date, status_month, status_quarter, status_year, days_in_status, "__metadata_run_id", "__metadata_run_timestamp"
FROM qedtherapeutics.substatus_utilization
union all
SELECT ic_transaction_id, longitudinal_patient_id, pharmacy_parent_name, brand, referral_date, status_date, status, substatus, ship_date, status_month, status_quarter, status_year, days_in_status, "__metadata_run_id", "__metadata_run_timestamp"
FROM qedtherapeutics.substatus_utilization
except
SELECT ic_transaction_id, longitudinal_patient_id, pharmacy_parent_name, brand, referral_date, status_date, status, substatus, ship_date, status_month, status_quarter, status_year, days_in_status, "__metadata_run_id", "__metadata_run_timestamp"
FROM helsinn.substatus_utilization'''

DISPENSE Assessment:

Correct File Names:
Expected file name is IntegriChain_Hutchmed_Sevsury_Daily_SPDispense_YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS.txt.    Extract shows   IntegriChain_ONCO360_IC_[DRUG]_SP_DISPENSE_20220411_181306.txt


LONGITUDINAL_PATIENT_ID – LPID column is blank in both UAT and PROD


PATIENT_CONSENT_DATE:  Format is YYYYMMDD.  Extract shows DD-MM-YYYY
  

PRIOR_AUTH_START_DATE:  Format is YYYYMMDD.  Extract shows DD-MM-YYYY


PRIOR_AUTH_EXPIRATION_DATE: Format is YYYYMMDD.  Extract shows DD-MM-YYYY
 

The following column headers are lowercase in extract and should be uppercase:
PRIMARY_PAYER_BIN
PRIMARY_PAYER_PCN
PRIMARY_PAYER_GROUP_ID
PRIMARY_PAYER_IIN
SECONDARY_PAYER_NAME
SECONDARY_PAYER_BIN
SECONDARY_PAYER_PCN
SECONDARY_PAYER_GROUP_ID
SECONDARY_PAYER_IIN
 

RX_NUMBER_OF_REFILLS – For this field we have an INTEGER values in the extract

from io import FileIO
import os
from typing import List
import pandas as pd
import yaml

tables = [

    # 'patient_dispensfirst_status_reporte_mastered',
    # 'patient_dispense_refined',
    # 'patient_dispense_mastered'
    # 'patient_journey_permutations',
    'patient_status_dispense_mastered'
    # 'patient_status_mastered'
    # 'patient_status_pdc_gap_days',
    # 'patient_status_portion_of_days_covered',
    # 'patient_status_refined',
    # 'patient_status_time_on_therapy',
    # 'patient_status_timeliness',
    # 'patient_status_ttff'
]
stream = FileIO('columns_to_skip.yml', 'r')
columns_to_skip = yaml.load(stream, Loader=yaml.FullLoader)
stream = FileIO('columns_to_sort.yml', 'r')
columns_to_sort = yaml.load(stream, Loader=yaml.FullLoader)


def download_tables(tables: List):
    folder_url = "s3://{env}-icdr-data/icdr-{env}/apellis/empaveli/dimensional/{table}"

    for table in tables:
        # for env in ['nbstage', 'uat', 'prod']:
        for env in ['uat', 'prod']:
            inputfolder = folder_url.format(env=env, table=table)
            df_in = pd.read_parquet(inputfolder)
            table_name = "{table}_{env}".format(table=table, env=env)
            df_in.to_parquet(f"data/parquet/{table_name}.parquet")


def __load_parquet(file, columns_to_skip: List = []):
    df = pd.read_parquet(file)
    if len(columns_to_skip) > 0:
        df.drop(columns_to_skip, axis=1, errors='ignore', inplace=True)
    return df


def check_columns(table: str, columns_to_skip: List = []):
    df_prod = __load_parquet(f"data/parquet/{table}_prod.parquet", columns_to_skip)
    columns_prod = set(df_prod.columns)
    df_nbstage = __load_parquet(f"data/parquet/{table}_nbstage.parquet", columns_to_skip)
    columns_nbstage = set(df_nbstage.columns)
    prod_diff = list(columns_prod - columns_nbstage)
    if len(prod_diff) > 0:
        print("[WARNING] {table}_prod EXCEPT {table}_nbstage:".format(table=table))
        print(", ".join(sorted(prod_diff)))
    nbstage_diff = list(columns_nbstage - columns_prod)
    if len(nbstage_diff) > 0:
        print("[WARNING] {table}_nbstage EXCEPT {table}_prod:".format(table=table))
        print(", ".join(sorted(nbstage_diff)))

# def check_columns(table: str, columns_to_skip: List = []):
#     df_prod = __load_parquet(f"data/parquet/{table}_prod.parquet", columns_to_skip)
#     columns_prod = set(df_prod.columns)
#     df_uat = __load_parquet(f"data/parquet/{table}_uat.parquet", columns_to_skip)
#     columns_uat = set(df_uat.columns)
#     prod_diff = list(columns_prod - columns_uat)
#     if len(prod_diff) > 0:
#         print("[WARNING] {table}_prod EXCEPT {table}_uat:".format(table=table))
#         print(", ".join(sorted(prod_diff)))
#     uat_diff = list(columns_uat - columns_prod)
#     if len(uat_diff) > 0:
#         print("[WARNING] {table}_uat EXCEPT {table}_prod:".format(table=table))
#         print(", ".join(sorted(uat_diff)))


def diff_columns():
    for table in tables:
        print("Columns to Skip", columns_to_skip)
        check_columns(table, columns_to_skip[table])


def tables_to_csv():
    for table in tables:
        # for env in ['nbstage', 'uat', 'prod']:
        for env in ['uat', 'prod']:
            df = __load_parquet(f"data/parquet/{table}_{env}.parquet", columns_to_skip[table])
            df = df.reindex(sorted(df.columns), axis=1)
            if 'pharmacy_transaction_id' in df.columns:
                df['pharmacy_transaction_id'] = "'" + df['pharmacy_transaction_id'] + "'"
            sorted_file = f"data/csv/{table}_{env}.csv"
            if table in columns_to_sort:
                df.sort_values(columns_to_sort[table], inplace=True)
                df.to_csv(sorted_file, index=False)
            else:
                unsorted_file = f"data/csv/{table}_{env}.unsorted.csv"
                df.to_csv(unsorted_file, index=False, float_format='%.15f')
                os.system(f"(head -n 2 {unsorted_file} && tail -n +3 {unsorted_file} | sort) > {sorted_file}")
                os.system(f"rm -f {unsorted_file}")


def main():
    download_tables(tables)
    diff_columns()
    tables_to_csv()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
